  <script type="text/javascript"><!--
    function CocheAll() {
      var lst = $('.case').map(function(){return $(this).val();}).get().join(',');
      Coche(lst,1);
    }
    function Coche(id,all) {
      $.ajax({
	url: "ajax/checkinstitution.php",
	type: "POST",
	data: "id=" + id + "&all=" + all,
	cache: false,
	success:function(msg){
	  $("#tools").html(msg);
	  if ( !id ) $('.case').prop("checked", false);
	  if ( all ) $('.case').prop("checked", true);
	},
	error:function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrows){	// PB AJAX
	  $.fancybox('<p>AJAX ERROR</p>',{padding:15,closeBtn:true});
	}
      }); 
    }
  //--></script>
